## Text Elements
The Lorentz transformations were not
given by Einstein, but INTERPRETED
(of course, considering his own postulates
in mind) ^FTQweE9t

up until 20th CE, Galilean invariance considered TIME to be invariant across 
different reference frames and coordinate transformations.

That is what is different for relativity.
It considers time to be variant, and speed of light to be invariant ^gnpzvyjt

"rest
frame" ^hZ6V8STk

although,
really, anyone can claim they 
are at rest ^UZx307GZ

just like you have linear transformations that make the physical size and direction of a vector invariant
 irrespective of the coordinate axis,
Lorentz transformations transform events defined at (x,y,z,t) such that speed of light is invariant for all inertial frames of
reference. ^UByrONrS

so B<<1 gives
Galilean Relativity ^jkThzxQ6
